<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hearts.html>hearts</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">heart</i></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the four suits of playing cards, in red, marked with the symbol ♥.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A trick-taking card game in which players are penalized for taking <a href = vnd.unilang:hearts.html>hearts</a> and (especially) the queen of <a href = vnd.unilang:spades.html>spades</a>.</li></ol>

lang="sco">hadder</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">heddir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Heede</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:heather.html>heather</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:heathers.html>heathers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An evergreen plant, <i>Calluna <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i>, with spiky leaves and small purple, pink, or white flowers.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Ericaceae family.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Various species of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:erica.html>Erica</a></i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Various species of the genus <i>Cassiope</i>.</li>
<li>A purple colour with a tint of pink and blue.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:heather.html>heather</a> colour: <span style="background-color:915F6D; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">textiles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The use of interwoven yarns of mixed colours to produce flecks.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Calluna <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ling.html>ling</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">heath</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:heather.html>heather</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of a purple colour with a tint with pink and blue.</li></ol>

***hebbeding.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebbeding.html>hebbeding</a> (116927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to have</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ding.html>ding</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebbeding.html>hebbeding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebbeding.html>hebbedingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebbedingetje.html>hebbedingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> piece of junk</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gadget</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">gimmick</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">trinket</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">desirable but often depreciated commodity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***hebben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> (50)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have, to possess, own, hold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>Hebt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuut.html>minuut</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you <b>have</b> a minute?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezitten.html>bezitten</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be afflicted with a disease

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form the <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> tense of the active voice of most verbs, together with a past participle.</span>

***heben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heben.html>heben</a> (64814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:heben.html>heben</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:heven.html>heven</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:heven.html>heven</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hevan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*habbjan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kh₂pyé-</i>, from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">heave</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hæve</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hieven.html>hieven</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:lift.html>lift</a>; to raise</li>

***heden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a> (4533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hude</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">huden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hiudo</i>, a contraction of the instrumental phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hiu dago</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on this day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The appearance of the vowel <i>-e-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unusual, the expected form in modern Dutch would be <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*<a href = vnd.unilang:huiden.html>huide</a>(n)</i>, compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huidig.html>huidig</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hiudu</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hūdigu</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">heute</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hjoed</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hēodæg</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>the present</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hedendages</i>, originally an adverb. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hedendag</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i>.

***heel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> (130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hēl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hailaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heler.html>heler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>complete, full, whole</li>
<li>unbroken, undamaged, untarnished</li>
<li>big, enormous, significant</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volledig.html>volledig</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heil.html>heil</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>very</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Although an adverb, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></i> may be inflected as well (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></i>) to match the following adjective, by analogy with the inflection of adjectives in Dutch.
</p><p>. For example, both of these sentences are correct:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>very</b> large tree.</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>very</b> large tree.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<p>The latter form may be regarded as informal and less appropriate for formal writing.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***heen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a> (280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:henen.html>henen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">away from here, hence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>away
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:baron.html>baron</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaf.html>gaf</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:koetsier.html>koetsier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wenk.html>wenk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rijtuig.html>rijtuig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rolde.html>rolde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:baron.html>baron</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> the coachman a sign and the carriage rolled <b>away</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to, towards
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>Waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></b>?</i>
<dl><dd>Where am I going?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a>, outside the boundaries of the <a href = vnd.unilang:norms.html>norms</a>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already too far <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a></b>. (could imply being drunk or having <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> his mind)</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***heer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a> (762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hērro</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hēro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hēriro</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hērro</i>, the comparative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hēr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noble, venerable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hehr</i>), by analogy with Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senior</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">elder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The Old High German word originally meant "grey, grey-haired", and descends from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hairaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, making it cognate with English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hoar</i>, Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hárr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heren.html>heren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heertje.html>heertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lord; master</li>
<li>gentleman</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">here</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">heri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harjaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***heersen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heersen.html>heersen</a> (6553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêerschen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to command, rule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">herrschen</i> (Early New High German).  Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heersen.html>heersen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to rule</li>
<li>to prevail
<dl><dd><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heerste.html>heerste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onbeschrijfelijk.html>onbeschrijfelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wanorde.html>wanorde</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>An indescribable <a href = vnd.unilang:chaos.html>chaos</a> prevailed in the room before him.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:heersen.html>heersen</a></b>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hēt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haitaz</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a> (10509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habjaną</i>, a class 6 strong verb with j-present, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kh₂pyéti</i>, from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heft</a> (12303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hefte</i>. Forms with <i>-cht-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> dominant in Middle Dutch. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heft</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heften</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heftje.html>heftje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>handle of a knife or other tool, haft, hilt</li>
<li>(<i>metaphor, used absolutely</i>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heft</a></b>) control, charge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heft</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:handen.html>handen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> the show here.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gevest.html>gevest</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">handgreep</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heft</a></strong>

***heftig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heftig.html>heftig</a> (5302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>16th c., borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:heftig.html>heftig</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">heftec</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">heiftec</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">heiftig</i>. Can be analyzed as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heft</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">control</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heftig.html>heftig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heftiger.html>heftiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heftigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fierce, severe</li>
<li>violent</li>
<li>passionate</li>
<li>impetuous, impulsive</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hegge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hegga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*haggju</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hedge</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hecke</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kagʰyo-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kagʰyóm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enclosure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cohum</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">cae</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heid.html>heid</a> (32603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:heid.html>heid</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">heifd</i>, northern forms of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">heed</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">heved</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hēafod</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">head</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haubudą</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Haupt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">huvud</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kauput-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*káput-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caput</i>), a variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kapōlo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head, bowl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">heidin</i>, a substantivised form of the adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">heidin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pagan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heide.html>heide</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hei.html>hei</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kneuter</i>. The sense “bumpkin” may be due to association with unrelated <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">keuter</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">keuterboer</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bumpkin, yokel, <a href = vnd.unilang:hick.html>hick</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">unsophisticated rural person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***heimelijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heimelijk.html>heimelijk</a> (17497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Fom <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haimalīkaz</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">heim</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">heem</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimlich.html>heimlich</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">heimelik</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">homely</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hemmelig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimelijk.html>heimelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimelijk.html>heimelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heimelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>secretive</li>
<li>furtive, stealthy
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steels.html>steels</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***heimlich.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heimlich.html>heimlich</a> (40726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimlich.html>heimlich</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">heimelich</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">heimilīh</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haimalīkaz</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Heim</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">-lich</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimelijk.html>heimelijk</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">homely</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hemmelig</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">hemlig</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">homely</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimlich.html>heimlich</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de">heimlicher</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am heimlichsten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>secret, clandestine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">done or kept in secret</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***hein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>hein</a> (22234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>hein</a></i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to physically demarcate lands</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:omheinen.html>omheinen</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>hein</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>heintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>physical demarcation between fields or <a href = vnd.unilang:yards.html>yards</a>, like a fence, wall or ditch.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a> (69673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A robbery or burglary, especially from an institution such as a bank or museum.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> August 21,  “A brazen <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a> in Paris  | print version: <i>International New York Times</i>, 22 August 2014, p. 8 | ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The New York Times">The New York Times</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/08/22/opinion/a-brazen-heist-in-paris.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The audacious hijacking in Paris of a <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> carrying the baggage of a Saudi prince to his private jet <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> obviously an embarrassment to the French capital, whose ultra-high-end <a href = vnd.unilang:boutiques.html>boutiques</a> have suffered a spate of <b>heists</b> in recent months.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fiction genre in which a <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> central to the plot.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b>,  <cite>Theatre Record</cite>, page 1177:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a conventional <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a></b> play in which the drama <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> created less through the characters' actions than through the fact of one of them having a gun.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2008</b> March 6, Robert Wilonsky, "Fast and Loose", <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Riverfront_Times" class="extiw" title="w:Riverfront Times">Riverfront Times</a></i> volume 32 number 10, page 28,
<dl><dd><i>The Bank Job</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the first proper Jason Statham movie since his days banging about in Guy Ritchie's early <b>heists</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  Daryl Lee,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>Heist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>Film</a>: Stealing With Style</cite>, page 69:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The crew resemble typical <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a></b> characters[.]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hēkelen</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hekelen.html>hekelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of flax</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heckle, to comb with a hackle (heckling comb)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to satirise, to lampoon</li></ol>

***hel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a> (910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:helle.html>helle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hella</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haljō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover, hide, conceal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellen.html>hellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>helletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Hell, an infernal afterlife.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I hope you will burn in <b>hell</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poel.html>poel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">jammerpoel</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A terrible place or ordeal.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakte.html>maakte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarmee.html>daarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>With that he made her life into a <b>hell</b>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hell</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hela.html>hela</a> (27131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanhilaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hiele</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiel.html>hiel</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">hēla</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hæll</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hæl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">häl</i>).
</p>
